[DocumentBodyStart:10932cc0-1434-41ad-bcf3-0b4841fd7f8e] --><div class=\"jive-rendered-content\"><p><span style=\"font-family: 'helvetica neue', helvetica, arial, 'lucida grande', sans-serif;\">As part of G5's ongoing commitment to Security, G5 IT will enable Okta's multifactor authentication (</span><span class=\"il\" style=\"font-family: 'helvetica neue', helvetica, arial, 'lucida grande', sans-serif;\">MFA</span><span style=\"font-family: 'helvetica neue', helvetica, arial, 'lucida grande', sans-serif;\">) feature when accessing Okta \"Off Network\"; e.g. coffee shop, home or airport.&#160; Any Okta login attempt outside of the G5 network will be met with the standard <span style=\"font-family: 'helvetica neue', helvetica, arial, 'lucida grande', sans-serif; color: #000000;\">username and password</span> followed by a second authentication method such as a personal security question and answer.&#160; You will be required to setup an MFA method the first time you attempt to access Okta \"Off Network\".</span></p><p style=\"min-height: 8pt; padding: 0px;\">&#160;</p><p><span style=\"text-decoration: underline; font-size: 12pt;\"><strong>What is Multifactor Authentication (MFA)?</strong></span></p><p style=\"min-height: 8pt; padding: 0px;\">&#160;</p><p style=\"padding-left: 30px;\">Multifactor authentication (MFA) is a security practice that requires more than one method of authentication to verify the user's identity for a login or transaction.</p><p>&#160;&#160;&#160; </p><ul><ul><li>Security question and answer</li><li>Text message containing security codes</li><li>Mobile phone authentication applications such as Google Authenticator or Okta Verify</li></ul></ul><p style=\"min-height: 8pt; padding: 0px;\">&#160;</p><p><span February 1st, 2017</p><p style=\"min-height: 8pt; padding: 0px; padding-left: 30px;\">&#160;</p><p><span style=\"text-decoration: underline; font-size: 12pt;\"><strong>What do I have to
